Local News

The National Postal Workers' Union Holds Its General Assembly; Opening Ceremony Held Yesterday Morning... Preparatory Meeting Held in the Afternoon... 90

The National Postal Workers' Union held the opening ceremony of its Third National Congress at the Ningbo Tongxiang Association on Xizang Road at 10:00 a.m. yesterday. A preparatory meeting was held in the afternoon. The venue was very tidy, and the delegates from various places participated enthusiastically. Details are as follows:

Attending Delegates

Changsha: Zhang Rongqing, Tao Xianpeng; Fuzhou: Zhang Fubao, Chen Danian, Wang Yaoting, Lin Guozhen; Yantai: Chen Changrong; Hankou: Yin Zichao, Luo Liting, Peng Weizhen, Han Dayong; Changde: Yu Renjie; Hangzhou: Zai Tingxian, Ma Wenyuan; Yin County: Han Wenzao; Jiangdu: Jin Jiemei; Shantou: Sun Dakun, Xu Shaowen; Nanchang: Xin Ganggang, Li Zhaolin; Jiujiang: Li Zhaoyu; Shanghai: Zhang Yidao, Fan Caicong, Shui Xiangyun, Lu Guangming; Qingdao: Hong Yongzhi, Wang Yongnian; Huaining: Zhang Yuren; General Union: Lu Shigao, Zhao Shusheng, Lu Jingshi, Zhu Xuefan, Zhang Kechang, Cheng Zuoqing, Kong Fanzao, Wang Kai, Wang Xuansheng, Tang Jiaxiu; Wu County: Wei Delin; Nanjing: Cai Yiling; Jinan: Jiang Shuli, Huang Zhaoguang; Yan County: Zhang Yongxian; Kaifeng: Zhang Guangdai, Zhao Yanqi; Tongshan: Han Dezhen; Luoyang: Jiang Zhongqi; Xichuan: Zheng Tingjie; Bojiang: Wang Yide; Tianjin: Zhang Yizhi; Wujin: Jiang Yuhuan; Wuxi: Mi Fenglu; Guangzhou: Zhao Heng, Liang Jiu; Wuhu: Gu Lide, Ye Yunhan, Li Fahe; Zhengzhou: Zhang Yongxian; Xiamen: Chen Yungong; Fuzhou: Wang Yaoting; and guests: Zhou Muyi of the China Seamen's Union, Cheng Haifeng of the National Labor China Branch, Lin Meiyan of the Municipal Party Department, Jiang Yiping of the Lawyers Association, Ren Jinpin of the Local Association, Wang Xiaolai of the Municipal Council, Wang Jiashu of the China Labor Association, Zhou Xuexiang of the Municipal Federation of Trade Unions, and more than 200 others.

Report by Mr. Lu

After the formal ceremony, Chairman Lu Jingshi gave a report, stating briefly: "Our association held the first National Postal Workers' Congress in Shanghai on December 1, 1929. Although it was very simple on the surface, it was very inspiring in spirit. On July 21, 1932, we held the second Congress in Nanjing. Today, we are holding the third Congress in this city. The original articles of association stipulated that a Congress should be held every two years, but due to various reasons, the Executive Committee of the General Union decided to postpone it for two years. In today's meeting, the delegates participating are very enthusiastic, and the delegates from all over the country, thousands of miles away, have come from afar to participate, which is deeply gratifying. In today's meeting, there are also postal worker representatives from several provinces in the Northeast, which makes people feel infinitely sad. When we hold the National Congress here, on the one hand, we should review everything ourselves, such as how to improve and correct the past association affairs, how to seek continuous development for our own welfare, and how to seek soundness in postal affairs. I hope that all delegates can contribute their opinions as much as possible. At the same time, we see that the current national crisis in our country is serious. The seriousness of the national crisis is due to the pressure exerted by imperialism and the constraints of various unequal treaties. However, we look around the world at countries such as Soviet Russia, Italy, and Germany. In this complex and severe international situation, under the leadership of a sound leader, they have broken away from all constraints and become powerful in the world. Our country must also have a leader to lead the entire nation to fight for national salvation. We also recall that in the recent revolutionary history of China, after Chairman Chiang Kai-shek led the revolutionary soldiers to the successful Northern Expedition, he also severely suppressed the communist bandits. During this period when the country was in an extremely serious situation due to various relations, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek remained tireless and maintained the Chinese nation in this difficult and arduous situation. Therefore, if we want to seek national salvation and survival, abolish unequal treaties, and recover lost territories, we can only support Chairman Chiang Kai-shek as our leader to lead the entire nation to fight." (Applause from everyone) Finally, today we are holding this Congress here. The spring is bright and the weather is warm, so this association will discuss all association affairs and will be able to cooperate sincerely and achieve bright and upright results.

Speech by Mr. Lin

Lin Meiyan, the representative of the Municipal Party Department, said in his speech, "I am very happy to participate in this grand meeting today. The soundness of your association's organization and the excellence of its members are truly superior to all other trade unions in the country. However, I hope that your association should take the responsibility of leadership so that all other trade unions in the country can regard this as a model and also tend to be sound and excellent. Just now, the chairman mentioned that to save China's crisis, we must wait for the leader's guidance. The leader is like the brain of a person. Without a brain, all actions will lose their direction and become unconscious. If the human organization is like this, why is the national organization not so? The brain of the country is a hard-working and meritorious leader. Mussolini of Italy, Hitler of Germany, and Stalin of Soviet Russia are absolutely worshiped and believed by the people of each country. Therefore, each country can be of one mind to seek the development of the country and the nation. Today, China has Chairman Chiang Kai-shek who has dedicated himself to the country and fought for the nation. He is the only leader of China today. The people of our country should unanimously support Chairman Chiang Kai-shek to lead the entire nation and work hard for national salvation and survival. Your association is the most sound and excellent trade union in our country, and all industrial circles regard it as a model, so you should call out from a high place and make all industrial circles follow your association to seek survival for the nation and seek revival for the country."

Speeches by Mr. Wang and Mr. Cheng

Wang Xiaolai, Speaker of the Municipal Council, said in his speech, "I am deeply honored that your association is holding its third Congress today with such vigorous spirit and enthusiasm. I have always regarded the postal workers' union in my mind as an organized and disciplined trade union, but trade unions should be feared by the general public. I think this kind of fear is a good phenomenon because of the manifestation of its strength. However, this kind of strength should not be shown to the people of the country, but should be shown to foreigners. In the future, your colleagues should also know and act in unison so that you will not be regarded by others as merely chanting high-sounding slogans. All the slogans in the venue today can be realized one by one." Cheng Haifeng of the International China Labor Bureau said in his speech, "The soundness of your association's organization has been recognized by the general public. I have inspected the labor situation in China. With the introduction of the person in charge of your association, I was able to contact the postal workers' unions in various parts of the country with great convenience, which shows the strictness of your association's organization. I hope that your association will continue to work hard for this purpose." Ren Jinpin of the Local Association and Zhou Xuexiang of the General Federation of Trade Unions also gave speeches. The length of the speeches is omitted.

Chairman's Big Thanks

Finally, Chairman Lu Jingshi gave a reply, saying briefly: "I am deeply grateful for the guidance of the representatives of the superiors and the encouragement of the guests today. In the future, this association will work harder and seek the happiness of the country and society."

The chairman first gave a report, stating briefly that the chairman group should be elected first in the preparatory meeting, and then the chairman would introduce the members of the proposal review committee of each group and draw the seats of each table. The staff of the conference should also be officially recognized. Then, the secretariat reported the number of delegates attending and the congratulatory telegrams from various places. The reply regarding the request to the Ministry of Transportation for the return of the flood donation was one by one.

French Female Journalist Dieta Nashi Arrives in Shanghai 91

According to the Outer Comments Section of the Continental News, Madame Dieta Nashi, a well-known French female journalist, after touring Japan and Northeast China, arrived in Shanghai by plane from North China the day before yesterday, and plans to return to Paris by plane on Tuesday (17th). According to her, when she arrived in Tokyo, it coincided with the military coup, and martial law was declared throughout the city. She also said that she had met with many Japanese political leaders in Japan. After receiving news of the Japanese incident in Shanghai, Die bought a ferry ticket to Japan, hoping to witness the situation in Tokyo at that time and provide news to her home country newspaper. When she arrived in Tokyo, the area was still under martial law, and someone told her that she could not leave the station and could only turn back. Die asked to make a phone call to the French embassy to tell them what had happened. The embassy agreed to send a car to the station to welcome her and told her that everything could be arranged. Soon after, she went to the embassy. At that time, French expatriates living in Tokyo, fearing outside disturbances, were all sheltering in the embassy. It is said that the situation at the U.S. Embassy was also similar. When the incident was not settled, more than 80 American expatriates all stayed at the embassy. Madame Die saw that there was no danger locally and went out to investigate for news purposes and interviewed many important Japanese figures. When she had time, she telegraphed everything to Paris for reporting. After order was restored in Tokyo, Madame Die decided to leave and took a plane to Changchun, Manchukuo. She saw that the people there were even more alarmed by the Tokyo incident than the citizens of Tokyo. In Changchun, she met with Puyi. She then left Manchukuo and went to Beiping, where she saw that the people there were all uneasy about the future. After staying for a few days, she came to Shanghai and is now scheduled to take a plane to Guangzhou on Tuesday, the 17th. After arriving in Guangzhou, she plans to hire a plane to Hanoi, and then take a French plane to Bangkok, and then transfer to a Dutch-British Airways plane to return to Paris.

Bank Draft Acceptance House Established Today and Begins Operations. Committee Established, Headed by Zhu Boquan as Manager. Thirty-Two Banks Join as Members, Subscribing to Membership Fees and Entering Agreements to Accept Drafts. 92

In recent years, the Shanghai market has been extremely depressed due to the outflow of silver, financial panic, and other influences. General industry and commerce, because transactions usually rely on credit, face only accounts receivable that cannot be turned into liquid assets during economic downturns. The financial industry, also due to the stagnation of capital use, cannot but engage in contraction, leading to a further tightening of the market, and the decline of industry and commerce becomes more apparent. The Shanghai Banking Association Joint Reserve Committee, recognizing this, proposed the organization of a bill acceptance house last March and April to add a credit instrument to the financial market and seek the flexibility of funds. At that time, discussions were held several times, but due to various reasons, it could not be realized immediately. This year, the association believed that the promotion of acceptance business could not be delayed any longer, and recently, in accordance with the resolution of the Shanghai Banking Association, it organized the Bank Draft Acceptance House to handle the draft acceptance business among banking colleagues, formulating seven chapters and thirty-three articles. The preparatory procedures have now been completed, and it is publicly announced today that it is established and will begin operations from today. Mr. Zhu Boquan concurrently serves as the manager of the house. In addition to the manager as an ex-officio member, an acceptance house committee of eleven members is established to handle the design of all affairs of the acceptance house and the formulation of various rules. The address is located at No. 59 Hong Kong Road, inside the Joint Reserve Committee. The details are recorded as follows:

Thirty-Two Member Banks

The member banks of the Shanghai Joint Reserve Committee and the clearing banks are eligible to join the house as member banks. As of the day before yesterday, the member banks that have joined, in addition to the Bank of China, Bank of Communications, and Postal Savings Bureau, etc., as special member banks, include Zhejiang Industrial Bank, Zhejiang Industrial Bank, Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank, the Four Banks Joint Savings Society, Yien Yieh Commercial Bank, Kincheng Banking Corporation, the Continental Bank, China & South Sea Bank, China Products Bank, the China National Bank of Commerce, Chung Foo Union Bank, the Agricultural & Industrial Bank of China, China Industrial Bank, Ningpo Commercial Bank, the China General Chamber of Commerce Bank, the Kiangsu Bank, the Sin Hua Trust, Savings & Commercial Bank, Wing On Bank, China Banking Corporation, The Chinese Industrial & Agricultural Bank, The Bank of Communications and Harmony, The Chuyuen Sincere Bank, The China State Bank, Banque Franco-Chinoise pour le Commerce et l'Industrie, The National Industrial Bank of China, The Silk Industry Bank, Shanghai Women's Commercial & Savings Bank, The Local Bank of Chekiang, Sichuan Mei Feng Bank, Jiangsu Farmers Bank, The Wing Tai Industrial Bank, and Heng Li Bank, a total of thirty-two. Members who join the member banks, except for special member banks, subscribe to the house's draft acceptance fund in proportion to their capital surplus. This fund must be paid in full at the time of joining. The membership fee is divided into three types: 1,000 yuan, 500 yuan, and 300 yuan, and each bank selects one on its own.

Official Announcement of Establishment Today

Bank Draft Acceptance House Public Announcement No. 1 states: This house is entrusted by the Shanghai Banking Association and resolved by the Shanghai Joint Reserve Committee member bank representatives to handle the draft acceptance business among banking colleagues. Banks have joined and subscribed to sufficient funds. It is now organized and established and will begin operations on March 16, 25th year of the Republic. This is hereby announced. Manager Zhu Boquan, Deputy Manager Xu Baoqi, Assistant Manager Kong Bao Cheng, Ye Chunquan, Address: 59 Hong Kong Road.

Purpose of Establishing a Draft Acceptance House

Bank Draft Acceptance House Articles of Association, approved by the 14th resolution of the Committee Member Bank Representatives Conference on February 20, 25th year of the Republic. Chapter 1, General Provisions, Article 1, The Shanghai Banking Association Joint Reserve Committee (hereinafter referred to as "the Committee") establishes a bill acceptance house in accordance with the resolution of the Shanghai Banking Association to develop agriculture, industry, and commerce and promote the discount business of the banking industry, and handles bank bill acceptance matters. Article 2, The external name of the house is designated as "Bank Draft Acceptance House" (hereinafter referred to as "the House"). Article 3, The draft acceptance fund of the house is subscribed by member banks, and a separate public agreement is made. Article 4, Member banks bear joint responsibility for the acceptance business of the house in proportion to the amount of the draft acceptance fund subscribed, within the total amount.

Payment of Membership Fees and Acceptance Funds

Chapter 2, Member Banks, Article 5, All member banks and clearing banks of the Committee are eligible to join the house as member banks. Article 6, When joining, member banks should fill out an application form and submit it to the house for record, and sign the public agreement stipulated in Article 3. Article 7, When joining, member banks should independently determine one of the following membership fees and pay it to the house: National Currency One

Page 12

Thousand Yuan, National Currency Five Hundred Yuan, National Currency Three Hundred Yuan. Article 8, When joining, member banks should pay in full the draft acceptance fund subscribed to. Article 9, Member banks may not withdraw from the house unless they provide a reason and are approved by the Committee Member Bank Representatives Conference. Article 10, Even if a member bank withdraws, it is still liable for the acceptance business conducted by the house before the withdrawal in accordance with Article 4 of these Articles of Association. Article 11, When a member bank withdraws from the house, its deposited draft acceptance fund should be returned by the house after the liability stipulated in Article 4 of these Articles of Association is extinguished. Article 12, When the Committee Member Bank Representatives Conference discusses draft acceptance matters, member banks that have not joined as member banks or have withdrawn have no voting rights.

Separate Evaluation and Management Groups

Chapter 3, Staff, Article 13, The Committee establishes a Bill Acceptance House Committee to discuss and consult with the Executive Committee of the Committee to handle the draft acceptance affairs of the house. Article 14, The Bill Acceptance House Committee consists of twelve members, of which eleven are elected by the Committee Member Bank Representatives Conference from the important staff of the member banks, and the manager of the Committee is an ex-officio member. Their term of office is one year, except for ex-officio members, and they may be re-elected. Article 15, The Bill Acceptance House Committee consists of five standing committee members, who are appointed by the Executive Committee of the Committee from the members other than the ex-officio members, to consult with the Standing Committee of the Committee and assist in handling the daily affairs of the house. Article 16, The Bill Acceptance House Committee establishes the following two groups: Guarantee Evaluation Group, Guarantee Management Group, Each group has several members, and the Bill Acceptance House Committee elects one member as the chairman of the group, and the other members are appointed by the Bill Acceptance House Committee and hired by the house.

Types of Acceptance Guarantees

Chapter 4, Acceptance Business, Article 17, The house's acceptance of drafts is limited to those issued by member banks. Member banks shall submit a contract to the house and deliver to the house property and goods approved by the house as the guarantee for the face value. Article 18, The acceptance guarantees are limited to the following types: Various major domestic products. The types of goods in the previous item are determined by the Executive Committee of the Committee from time to time. Drafts. The due date shall not exceed ninety days from the date of acquisition by the house and shall be signed by one member bank. Commercial drafts payable abroad. The due date of the previous drafts shall not exceed ninety days from the date of acquisition by the house and shall be signed by one member bank. Government bonds, corporate bonds, and stocks with market prices. The previous stocks refer to the stocks of limited companies other than member banks. Real estate in this city (limited to those with income). Other goods and properties approved by the Executive Committee of the Committee. Article 19, When the house receives the goods and properties stipulated in the preceding article as acceptance guarantees, the proportion of each type of goods and properties in the total acceptance guarantees shall be determined by the Executive Committee of the Committee from time to time, but the properties stipulated in the fourth item of the preceding article shall not exceed 50% of the total acceptance guarantees, and the properties stipulated in the fifth item shall not exceed 25% of the total acceptance guarantees. Article 20, The total amount of acceptance for each member bank by the house shall be determined by the Executive Committee of the Committee from time to time. Article 21, The due date of the drafts accepted by the house shall not exceed ninety days from the date of issuance. Article 22, The discount on the guarantees for the drafts accepted by the house shall be determined by the Bill Acceptance House Committee from time to time, but the acceptance amount shall not exceed 75% of the evaluation of the guarantees. Article 23, The handling fee for the house's draft acceptance shall be determined by the Committee's reporting to the Executive Committee from time to time, but the minimum amount shall be 2.5 per mille (i.e., 2.5 jiao per thousand yuan) for every ten days based on the face value. If it is less than ten days, it shall also be calculated as ten days. Article 24, The following matters may be entrusted by the house to various member banks and other companies or groups. Member banks are obliged to act as agents when entrusted by the house: Inspection of acceptance guarantees. Payment of acceptance drafts upon maturity. When the issuing bank fails to fulfill the contract and the guarantee must be disposed of for compensation, the transportation and sale of the property.

Discounting and Rediscounting of Drafts

Chapter 5, Discounting and Rediscounting, Article 25, The drafts accepted by the house may be bought, sold, and discounted in the market, and if necessary, the Committee may be requested to discount them. Article 26, The drafts discounted by the member banks of the house in the preceding article may be rediscounted by the member banks requesting the Central Bank of China and the Bank of Communications if necessary. Article 27, The discount rate for the drafts accepted by the house shall be determined and announced by the Committee on a daily basis. Chapter 6, Accounting, Article 28, The house shall conduct final accounts on June 30 and December 31 of each year. The annual final accounts shall prepare the following reports and submit them to the Committee Member Bank Representatives Conference for approval by the Executive Committee of the Committee: Business Report, Balance Sheet, Property Catalog, Profit and Loss Statement, Proposal for the Appropriation of Public Reserve and Profit and Loss. Article 29, If there is net profit after the annual final accounts of the house, the public reserve shall be appropriated as a priority. Article 30, The profit and loss after the annual final accounts of the house, in addition to the provisions of the preceding article, shall be allocated in proportion to the amount of the draft acceptance fund subscribed by the member banks in the total amount. Chapter 7, Supplementary Provisions, Article 31, The various detailed rules for the house shall be formulated separately by the Committee. Article 32, If there are any matters not covered in these Articles of Association, they may be amended at any time. Article 33, These Articles of Association shall be implemented after being resolved by the Committee Member Bank Representatives Conference, and the same shall apply to amendments.

Silver Industry Holds Same Opinions on Interest Rate Reduction Plan 93

Believes National Banks Must First Provide Low-Interest Loans

Otherwise, There is Risk of Capital Flight from Various Banks and Firms

The Silver and Banking Industries Associations have been ordered by the Ministry of Finance to properly discuss reducing deposit and loan interest rates. The Banking Association has formed a subcommittee to study the matter, and the Silver Industry Association has entrusted the Executive Committee to study it. Both have now drafted measures and will soon consult with each other and report to the Ministry of Finance. According to the New Voice News Agency, the measures proposed by the Silver and Banking Industries Associations share the same opinions. They both believe that to reduce loan interest rates, national banks must first provide low-interest loans to their counterparts. Regarding reducing deposit interest rates, they believe that serious consideration should be given, otherwise, there is a risk of capital flight from various banks and firms. As it stands, the highest deposit interest rate for various banks and firms is no more than 1% per annum, while investing in bonds yields 1% per month.

Bank of Communications and Qihong Tea Cooperative Sign Loan Contract 94

Amount of 500,000 Yuan

According to the National News Agency, Hu Haochuan, Director of the Qimen Tea Improvement Farm, which is jointly organized by the Agricultural Department of the National Economic Council, the Central Agricultural Experiment Station of the Ministry of Industry, and the Anhui Construction Department, arrived in Shanghai yesterday with Hu Shiqi, a representative of the Anhui Provincial Finance Department, and Duan Tianjue, a representative of the Construction Department. Shaanxi Disaster Relief Bond Mortgage Loan Contract Signed 95

Totaling 240,000 Yuan, Term of Half a Year, Weekly Interest of 1%

Three Banks Undertake to Lend Money and Remit to Xi'an Branch for Payment

The Shaanxi Provincial Government, using 400,000 yuan of disaster relief bonds allocated by the Central Government, mortgaged 240,000 yuan in cash to the Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications at a 60% discount. The Shaanxi Provincial Government sent a representative, Yan Jingzhai, to Shanghai to negotiate with the three banks. After reaching an agreement, the loan contract was formally signed on the 13th of this month at the Shaanxi Provincial Government in Xi'an. The term is six months, with a weekly interest rate of 1%. The Central Bank of China and the Bank of China each recognize 96,000 yuan, and the Bank of Communications recognizes 48,000 yuan. The Xi'an branches of the three banks have reported the signing process to their Shanghai head offices. The borrowed funds will be remitted from Shanghai to Shaanxi within a few days to be fully paid in order to provide disaster relief to the victims in northern Shaanxi as soon as possible.

Chairman of the Money Industry Association, He Zhongxiao, Passed Away Due to Illness 102

Funeral Held at 8:00 AM This Morning

He Zhongxiao, Chairman of the Shanghai Money Industry Association, a native of Songxia, Shangyu, Zhejiang, enjoyed a high reputation in the financial community. He was the General Manager of Zikang Money House at the intersection of Tianjin Road and Henan Road in this city. He was usually very kind and amiable to people and things, and was kind-hearted and charitable. Since the third member meeting was held on October 2 of last year, he was elected as the chairman. He devoted much effort to the rectification of the association affairs, and all the members of the money industry celebrated that they had obtained a suitable person. However, due to overwork, he suffered from a long-term illness in January of this year, and the medicine was ineffective. He suddenly passed away on the morning of the day before yesterday at ten o'clock, at the age of forty-eight. Since the association heard the sad news of the death of Chairman He, in addition to flying the flag at half-mast for three days from yesterday, it also sent separate letters to all executive and supervisory committee members and member firms yesterday, stating that they would gather at He's residence at 7:30 AM this morning to pay their respects. The letter said: Respected Sir, Mr. He Zhongxiao, Chairman of the Committee of this Association, passed away on the 14th of March. The funeral will be held at Chen Shi on the 16th. Chairman He was the leader of this association. All who are in the same boat should go to pay their respects. Special notice is hereby given, and you are requested to go to He's residence at 4 Jueyuan, Aven Road, before 7:30 AM on the 16th to express your condolences.

China Institute of Technology Experiments with Remote Control Device Without Money 103

Fang Ziwei, Principal of the China Institute of Radio Engineering (also known as Radio Engineering) in this city, and Professor Yan, jointly advocated the manufacture of a wireless remote control device, and now announced that the experiment was successful, and the first public experiment was conducted the week before last. Checking that wireless remote control is currently being actively researched in various countries, the device advocated by Fang et al. is a prototype. If its power is increased, it can be applied to aircraft and military affairs. Its most outstanding feature is that it is a device for designating and remotely controlling any machine. Its operation is completely automatic and does not require manual labor. If the research is expanded in the future, it will make a great contribution to aviation and military equipment.

The Three Goodness Societies: Joint Deliberation on Condolences and Support for Sun Yinting 107

A few days ago, Chang Hui of the Shanghai Goods Relief Association for Earthquake Victims, along with Standing Committee members of various provincial Water Disaster Relief Associations, Zhu Qinglan, Wang Zhen, Qu Yingguang, Huang Qinglan, Cheng Jingsheng, Quan Shaowu, etc., after a meeting, specifically extended the time to propose that the reported suicide by drowning of relief worker Sun Yinting was deeply saddening. Relief colleagues planned to collect funds to assist the surviving family. A resolution was made: first, the Shanghai Water Disaster Relief Associations of various provinces, the Chinese Relief Society, and the Shanghai Taiwanese Disaster Relief Fund Management Committee, these three organizations, would send telegrams of condolence to the family and concurrently provide substantial assistance to help the family's living expenses. During the meeting, Cheng Jingsheng first reported on Sun's brief history. Sun Yinting, named Hongxiu, was from Baoying County, Jiangsu Province, and was almost fifty years old. He graduated from normal school, and although his classical Chinese wasn't great, he was very capable. Accounting and auditing were his strengths. He was particularly meticulous, and extremely responsible in his work. In the early years of the Republic of China, he worked as a staff member in the tax bureau under Wu Jingshan in Zhejiang, then followed Wu in disaster relief, enduring hardship and being both disciplined and excellent. Later, he worked under Liu Qusheng, Chen Borong, Qiao Mengqian, and others for the Shanghai Relief Association and the Shanghai Temporary Relief Association, traveling to various counties in Henan, Shaanxi, Zhejiang, Jiangsu, and other provinces for disaster relief inspections. He was kind-hearted, unafraid of hardship and danger, diligent in his duties, and honestly self-disciplined, refusing remuneration, which was respected by various charitable organizations. When Mr. Feng Menghua was in charge of the Shanghai Relief Association, he greatly appreciated him, so his reputation was quite prominent. He was commissioned to supervise the construction of the West Lake Villa for Hardoon Foreign Firm and went to Jiangxi to assist in tax affairs. At that time, he already felt economic hardship, speaking out frankly, a reversal of his former silence. He re-entered the Chinese Relief Society as a member, again handled Zhejiang relief efforts and river works, and the Taiwan disaster relief association hired him to manage the Ninghai project, achieving remarkable results, which was praised by the local community. During the 1931 flood, he was appointed as the inspection head for Funing and Xinghua by the National Government's Relief Committee for Water Disasters, the Jiangsu Provincial Relief Committee, the Shanghai fundraising for various provincial water disaster relief associations, and the Jiangsu Relief Association. He was overly eager to do things well, and he firmly refused any remuneration for disaster relief work. Even if colleagues occasionally gave assistance, he would be constantly concerned about it. After a long time of fulfilling obligations, his family's situation became increasingly difficult, and he suffered mental stress. Last year, he suddenly discussed with friends in Shanghai the possibility of trying to cultivate land west of Baoying Lake, hoping to solve his livelihood. The original plan did not meet expectations. He borrowed three to several thousand yuan from friends and returned home, but he did not listen to advice to seek another way of life, still reluctantly carrying out cultivation. In winter, the borrowed funds were insufficient, and he again sought help from others. This spring, building embankments in the reclamation area required a large amount of money. He came to Shanghai to visit friends and borrow money again. On the eighth of this month, he met them at the Grand Cathay Hotel, and he still looked calm, showing letters from friends advising him not to devote himself to reclamation, which may not be successful and may cause trouble. He said that his luck was bad and did not blame the reclamation land. He asked for help in borrowing money for consolidation. Jingsheng told him that the amount was too large and difficult to raise quickly, willing to give him some time to make plans. He thanked him and left, but unexpectedly, three days later, a newspaper had this shocking news. Mr. Feng Yangshan said that Mrs. Wu had also received a suicide note, stating briefly that the reclamation attempt had failed and that he had no choice but to end his life to apologize to friends. It is feared that it is already a tragic outcome, and there is deep sorrow. It is noted that his family has a wife, four young sons, and a daughter, all young and needing to be raised. It is proposed to ask colleagues to contribute generously. Next, Qu Yingguang spoke, saying that Mr. Sun was extremely sincere, and the various relief associations benefited greatly from his enthusiastic help. However, he had long been mentally disordered. When handling Taiwan relief, he demanded funds excessively. Although he was truly devoted to disaster relief, his awareness was too intense. That he would end up like this is painful. Colleagues should do their best to help. It was fitting to meet Mr. Feng Yangshan of the Chinese Relief Society who also had this intention and was very saddened. The three organizations should unite, and relief colleagues should take on the responsibility of raising condolence money separately. As for the body, having been thrown into the sea, it is impossible to retrieve. Then, the chairman Zhu Qinglan said that this gentleman was a good person, but inevitably stubborn. He had seen him several times before, and he certainly seemed to have a mental illness. It's a great pity. Wang Yiting said that a public appeal should be issued, and he could help first. Then, it was decided to raise money for condolences and also to request a commendation from the Central Relief Committee. Feng Yangshan and Cheng Jingsheng were publicly recommended to draft it.

Shanghai Land Bureau Announcement: Convenient Methods for Certificate Exchange 109

The Shanghai Land Bureau, in view of the fact that people holding single tax receipts to the bureau for certificate exchange cases are difficult to handle due to discrepancies in the single tax amount and also due to missing tax registers, making verification impossible, the handling of the above cases is quite difficult. The bureau has formulated flexible measures and issued a notice. The announcement (No. 24) of the Shanghai Land Bureau is recorded below: In the case of this bureau handling certificate exchange, the authenticity of the old tax receipts submitted by the people is reviewed, and the tax receipts submitted are checked to see if they correspond to the tax paid by the holder. If the single tax amount does not match, the certificate exchange will be hindered. Furthermore, there are cases where the tax registers presented in the register are carelessly stored, resulting in missing pages and sections, making it difficult to determine. If all certificate exchanges are not granted, then the land tax receipts held by the people are all evidence of property rights, and they will inevitably be disappointed. Moreover, in cases where the single tax amount does not match, the people have no way to adjust it themselves, and in cases where the tax register is missing, even if a thorough investigation is conducted, the previous tax registers and registers are regarded as private property and sold repeatedly, resulting in no basis for verification, and the matter is evaded. The bureau has difficulty in handling the above cases and has no fixed method to follow. Now, in order to facilitate certificate exchange, flexible measures are formulated and submitted to the municipal government for approval. All certificate exchange cases of the people, such as those where the tax register is missing and cannot be verified, or where the single tax amount does not match, but it is confirmed that they actually own the land, can be handled accordingly. The relevant measures are announced to the people of the city for their information. Specifically, the following are listed: Measures for collecting evidence for certificate exchange in cases where the tax register is missing or the single tax amount does not match: 1. The applicant must prove that they own the land in question. The method of proving it shall be to submit legal evidence of ownership. 2. In addition to submitting the evidence in the first item, if the land is leased, a lease agreement and lease tax must be submitted; if there are houses built on it, in addition to submitting a lease agreement and lease tax, a house tax receipt or construction permit must also be submitted. 3. For self-cultivated land or self-occupied houses, if the various evidences specified in the second item cannot be submitted, a guarantee shall be issued by two landowners with land certificates, or two reputable stores, or a joint guarantee from four neighbors. March 14, 25th year of the Republic of China, Cai Zengji, acting director.

The Chuannan Line of the Shangchuan Company: The Chuan-Zhu Section Had Its Opening Ceremony Yesterday — Plans to Connect to the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway in the Future — 110

The Shangchuan Transportation Co., Ltd., in order to develop the transportation between Shanghai, Chuansha, and Nanhui, has specifically expanded and built the Chuan-Zhu section of the Nanchuan County Road. This section has now been completed and a traffic opening ceremony was held yesterday. The details are recorded below.

Guests Attending: Those who attended yesterday went to Qingongtang in three groups. The first group departed from the Bund on Beijing Road by the city ferry to Qingning Temple at 9:00 AM, and then transferred to the company's special car. The second and third groups arrived at 10:00 AM and 11:00 AM respectively. There were a total of over eight hundred people, including representatives from the Nanhui County Party Headquarters Chen Shunping, the Chuansha County Party Headquarters Lu Shunqing, the Nanhui County Mayor Yuan Xiluo, and gentry, schools, institutions, and organizations from Chuannan. The company was represented by Chairman Qu ShaoYi, Manager Gu Bowei, and Gu Shuwei, among others. The presidium was composed of Yuan Xiluo, Qu ShaoYi, and Gu Bowei.

Opening Ceremony Circumstances

The opening ceremony was held as planned. First, Chairman Yuan Xiluo reported, stating briefly that today is the opening ceremony of the Chuan-Zhu section of the Nanchuan County Road of the Shangchuan Company. From now on, the transportation between Shanghai, Chuansha, and Nanhui will be more convenient, which is enough for the people of the three counties to rejoice. It was decided that the land foundation used by the Shangchuan Company was leased from the Nanhui County Government. In July of the 23rd year, the company, together with the Nanhui County Government, sent personnel to measure it. In December, it was approved by the Jiangsu Construction Department. On June 15th of the 24th year, the Nanhui County Government followed the contract to build the earthworks, which was completed in November, costing over 10,000 yuan in earthwork expenses and over 1,000 yuan in seedling subsidies. At the beginning of the road construction, the villagers had some misunderstandings. Thanks to the Nanhui and Chuansha County Party Committee members who organized a propaganda team to publicize to the people, there is today's success. This point should be thanked to the members of the two county party committees. In addition, there is a report that the farmland used for the road construction will be issued with a corresponding price starting from the first of next month.

Board Report

Subsequently, the chairman of the company, Qu ShaoYi, reported, stating briefly that our company was initiated in the 10th year of the Republic of China, and formally established in April of the 13th year, renting the county road to lay railway tracks and actively carrying out the work. On October 7th of the 14th year, a road rental and operation contract was signed. On the 8th of that month, the Qingning Temple to Gongjialu section was completed and opened to traffic. In January of the 15th year, the company, in order to extend the route, increased its capital by 150,000 yuan, combining with the old shares to a total of 300,000 yuan, building roads and laying tracks, continuing to work. In July of the same year, the Gongjialu to Sizhaogang section was completed, and the Shangchuan Road was fully opened to traffic. In June of the 18th year, the company's assets increased, and another 100,000 yuan of capital was raised, actively operating, leading to today. In the future, it is planned to extend the route to Fengxian, directly reaching the Shanghai-Hangzhou Highway.

Manager's Report

Subsequently, the manager of the company, Gu Bowei, reported on the company's operations, stating briefly that when our company first opened to traffic, there was only one black oil electric locomotive, two Ford locomotives, and five passenger cars. Later, as the number of passengers increased, we added one black oil locomotive and one oil electric locomotive each, and four passenger cars, and the business became more prosperous. Later, because these locomotives were too slow, the company, in order to improve, ordered three steam locomotives and six large passenger car chassis from Germany in October of the 19th year. In order to ensure traffic safety, we rebuilt wooden bridges into steel bridges in the 20th year. In September of the 22nd year, steam locomotives began to run. On May 15th of the 23rd year, the company ordered the lease and construction of the Chuanqin County Road from the Chuansha County Government, starting from Sizhao outside the north gate of Chuansha to the boundary of Qingongtang Nanhui County, a total of four kilometers. The Chuansha County Government was responsible for building the earthworks, while the company built steel bridges. The railway tracks were laid in October, and the entire line was opened to traffic on November 20th. When the Chuanqin Line was in progress, because the end point of this line was adjacent to the Nanhui border, if it were to connect with the Nanchuan County Road of Nanhui County in the future, the transportation of Shangnan and Chuan would be more convenient, and various businesses could obtain considerable development. Thanks to the support of all parties and local people in Nanhui, after several negotiations, a contract was signed with the Nanhui County Government in the shortest time to undertake the construction of the Nanchuan County Road and connect the tracks to traffic. In July of the 23rd year, the Nanhui County Government, together with the company, sent personnel to measure the road line. In December, it was approved by the Construction Department. On June 15th of the 24th year, the Nanhui County Government followed the contract to build the earthworks, focusing on the Chuan-Zhu section first, which was completed in November. The company immediately built steel bridges and laid railway tracks, which was completed last month. Therefore, the traffic opening ceremony is held today. Subsequently, Chen Songping, representative of the Nanhui County Party Committee, and Lu Shunqing, representative of the Chuansha County Party Committee, delivered speeches successively. At 1:00 PM, the meeting was adjourned.

Test Ride Circumstances

At 1:00 PM, the company's "opening ceremony special car," amidst military music and firecrackers, was opened for traffic by Mrs. Yuan cutting the ribbon. It arrived at Jiangzhen at around 1:20 PM and was suddenly blocked. The reporter got out of the car to observe and saw a white small flag in front, horizontally blocking the road, with the words "Jiangzhen People Request to Repave the Ballad Street" written on it. The reporter asked the residents of the town, who claimed that the Chuan-Zhu railway was passing directly through Jiangzhen Street, which was very inconvenient for pedestrians, so this request was made. Subsequently, the chairman of the company, Qu ShaoYi, discussed with the town mayor of the town. Because the company's road foundation was leased from the Nanhui County Government and had nothing to do with the company, the town mayor found a way to allow passage. After passing through Dengzhen and reaching Zhuqiao, all the guests got off the bus and were treated to lunch by the company. At 4:00 PM, the special car returned to Qingning Temple and boarded the city ferry back to Shanghai.

Central Savings Society: Officially Opens Today 111

The Central Savings Society, specially licensed by the National Government, has been allocated a fund of 5 million yuan by the Central Trust Bureau. The society's accounting is completely independent, and it has hired prominent financial figures in the country: Chen Xing, Li Ming, Chen Guangfu, Song Hanzhang, Qin Runqing, Du Yuesheng, Qian Xinzhi, Yu Qiaqing, Wang Xiaolai, Guo Bingwen, and Guo Shun, as members of the Supervisory Committee to supervise the use of savings and ensure the safety of depositors' interests. The manager of the society is Mr. Li Shuming, and the deputy managers are Zhu Shikang and Zhang Xisan. All old savings certificates of the Sino-French Savings Society that have been taken over can be exchanged for new certificates of the Central Savings Society after the opening. Today, the society officially starts business at No. 126 Hankou Road in this city. The Supervisory Committee will also convene its first meeting to discuss the matters in progress. It is also heard that the Minister of Finance, Kong Xiangxi, will also attend the meeting to give instructions. As for the savings offered by the society, there are various preferential measures for depositors. The main points of its articles of association are explained as follows: 1. The Society issues savings certificates with a face value of 2,000 yuan for the whole society, with a monthly saving of 12 yuan; 1,000 yuan for the half society, with a monthly saving of 6 yuan; 500 yuan for the quarter society, with a monthly saving of 3 yuan, until the face value is fully paid within 14 years. 2. Depositors who prepay savings for half a year can deduct 1 yuan per whole society, and those who prepay for one year can deduct 4 yuan. 3. The society holds a lottery draw every month, for a total of 180 draws within 15 years. In the last year, depositors do not need to pay savings but are still included in the lottery, with the hope of winning. 4. The calculation of the special prize amount is based on the number. It is 50,000 yuan when the number reaches 100,000. If it is less than 100,000, it will increase or decrease according to the certificate number. However, if it is less than 50,000, the prize money will be at least 29,000 yuan, and the difference will be supplemented by the society. 5. In addition to the special prize, every 2,000 certificates have a first prize of 2,000 yuan, a second prize of 300 yuan, a third prize of 200 yuan, and a fourth prize of 100 yuan, each one. Every 10 numbers have a last prize of 12 yuan, and there is also an additional prize. 6. When a depositor withdraws from the society midway, they can fully recover according to the withdrawal table. 7. Depositors can borrow from the society at any time after paying for two years. 8. Depositors who have paid in full can receive a full principal amount in addition to sharing a bonus. 9. The Society allocates half of the surplus from the income of the savings after deducting reserve funds to the bonus fund, generating compound interest. The bonuses that depositors who withdraw from the society midway do not issue as per the rules are also included in the interest accrual, so the bonus received by depositors when they have paid in full is exceptionally generous. 10. The Society's use of savings is handled in accordance with the safe methods stipulated in the articles of association, and it is reviewed by the supervisory committee. 11. During the lottery, it is handled under the supervision of the directors and supervisors of the Central Trust Bureau, the members of the Supervisory Committee of the Society, the auditing accountant, and the representatives of the depositors. (A detailed article of association is available upon request.)

The Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Communications, since receiving an order from the Ministry of Communications, ordered the Hankou Telephone Bureau to recruit five wireless radio female operators. Enthusiastic Registration

The bureau started the registration and oral examination for female operators on the 13th from 9:00 AM to 11:00 AM every day. By the closing deadline at noon on the 14th, a total of sixty-two people had registered and applied to participate in the oral examination. After the bureau's screening, only thirty-one people were qualified and were given examination permits to participate in yesterday's formal written examination.

Yesterday was the date of the formal examination. The examination was held on the second floor showroom and downstairs reception room of the bureau at Dananmen. Examination Conditions

The test questions in the morning were on Party Principles, Chinese, Arithmetic, and World Geography. The test ended at 12:00 noon. The six female operators selected by the Hankou Bureau must also be sent to Shanghai to receive the same three-month training. After the completion, all will be transferred to the Hankou Telephone Bureau for service.

Yihua Dance Troupe Lost Money: "Tears of Remorse" Film Mortgage Involved in Lawsuit 119

Hu Zhipei, a local resident, twenty-seven years old, residing at No. 85 Cihou Lane, An'nan Road, recently retained attorney Pan Renxi to file a criminal complaint in the Second Special Court against Yang Jinsheng for two counts of fraud and breach of trust. The main points of the complaint stated that the plaintiff organized the Yihua Dance Troupe in December last year and went to Suzhou, Shengze, Jiaxing, Pinghu and other ports to perform. As a result, business was sluggish and losses were quite heavy. The defendant, Yang Jinsheng, is the manager of the Shengze Grand Theater in Shengze Town. When going to various places to perform, the defendant introduced the troupe, resulting in a large accumulation of travel and meal expenses, which could not be paid. All of these expenses were advanced by the defendant. On January 8, the plaintiff settled accounts with the defendant at the Huifang Tea House on Wuma Road in the British Concession of Shanghai. The defendant advanced a total of twenty-eight yuan for the company. At that time, the plaintiff was unable to repay the amount and discussed with the defendant and agreed to convert the advance payment into a loan. The plaintiff used the recently produced "Tears of Remorse" film from the plaintiff's Zhaohua Film Company as collateral, specifying that the term of the mortgage loan was three months, during which the plaintiff could redeem the loan at any time. However, if the term expired and the loan was not redeemed, the defendant had the right to screen the film and use the proceeds to offset the principal and interest of the loan. However, the defendant should obtain the plaintiff's consent before screening the film in any theater. Unexpectedly, after the plaintiff prepared funds to redeem the loan, the defendant avoided meeting with the plaintiff. Moreover, the defendant dared to screen the film privately at the Fu'an Company, Xianshi Company, and Daqian World without obtaining the plaintiff's consent, renaming it "Tears of Remorse Shadow." When the plaintiff learned of this and protested, the defendant ignored the protest. The plaintiff requested that the defendant be investigated and prosecuted according to law. The defendant was summoned the day before yesterday afternoon. First, the plaintiff's attorney stated the previous circumstances and said that the plaintiff intended to redeem the film and send it to the Jin Cheng and other major theaters for screening. Now, the defendant sent it to a recreational ground for screening, which caused the film's value to decrease. When questioned, the defendant Yang Jinsheng claimed that the plaintiff had repeatedly delayed redemption, so he had no choice but to send it to various recreational grounds for screening in accordance with the provisions of the contract. However, the quality of the "Tears of Remorse" film was poor, and the screening was blurred and unclear, which was not welcomed by the audience. It was estimated that the Fu'an Company only screened it for one day, charging seven yuan and ten cents. The Xianshi Company charged forty yuan, and the Daqian World charged fifty yuan. The amount received was not enough to offset the debt. The merchant had declared to the guarantor Wang Weiqing during the screening, and Wang could testify in court. The attorney defended everything on behalf of the defendant. Witness Wang Weiqing testified that Yang Jinsheng did tell the merchant that the film was sent to the recreational ground for screening. Judge Zhang ordered the case to be adjourned for sentencing on the 19th.

Tao Longshun, a Can Manufacturer in Pudong, Was Twice Intimidated by Gangs 120

First, a Thief Was Arrested Who Claimed the Victim Was His Brother-in-Law

Then Three Accomplices Were Arrested and Sent to the Bureau for Interrogation

Tao Jinze, a Pudong resident, fifty-two years old, residing at No. 30 Tianbao Branch Road, Zhabei, operates the Tao Longshun Can Factory. The business is doing quite well. He was targeted by bandits. On the afternoon of the fifteenth of last month, at about 6 PM, a thug named Yan Shifu, leading three people, broke into Tao's bedroom, brandishing a handgun, and warned him not to make a sound. They demanded that he hand over two thousand dollars within three days, otherwise they would use the handgun. They then dispersed. After Tao received this alarming message, he immediately reported to the Linping Road Police Station in the Fifth District to request an arrest. The police station dispatched detective Zhang Liangjin to investigate. Unexpectedly, at 2 PM the day before yesterday, Tao was passing by the door of the Yangtie Store Quan Genhu on Tianshi Road in a car. Suddenly, Yan Shifu, leading many people, ambushed in the store, rushed out and stopped Tao's car, snatching a small Luzon wool hat (valued at sixteen yuan). At the same time, two thugs threw a bucket of urine and feces at Tao, splashing it all over his body. Yan Shifu shouted, "Today I'm sending you a message. If there is no reply within three days, I will shoot you dead." Tao again reported to the Detective Corps of the Public Security Bureau and the Linping Road Police Station, requesting that they be wanted. Then, at 5 PM on the same afternoon, a fellow villager, Yao Xiaomao, visited Tao Jinze's home. After talking, he told Tao that he had seen Yan Shifu, Lu Guirong, Xiao Fusheng, and Quan Genhu secretly discussing in a small inn near Linping Road, fearing that there would be further severe actions. Tao Jinze reported to the Detective Corps Chief Ji Yuanpu of the Public Security Bureau, who immediately dispatched the Ximen Squad Leader Li Xiaobao, leading detectives Liu Wenwen, Jin Yushan, etc., to No. 37 Zhenxiu Lane, Yangjiadu, Pudong, at about 4 AM yesterday. Yan Shifu was still sleeping and had not gotten up. When he knew that the detectives had arrived, he hid under the bed, but was eventually dragged out and arrested. He was taken to the Ximen Branch Bureau. Under interrogation, he confessed, "Tao Jinze is my brother-in-law. I threatened him with a handgun because of business issues, not to extort two thousand yuan. My accomplices Lu Guirong, Ni Fusheng, and Hua Fuquan are now at the Baoxing Hotel." The case handlers then went to the hotel and arrested Lu Guirong, Ni Fusheng (Xiao Fusheng), and Hua Fuquan (Hu Quan), three people. After interrogation at the bureau, the case was deemed to be a major case of extortion, so a document was prepared and sent to the General Bureau for reception.

Gao Yonglian Pays Fifteen Yuan per Month

Gao Shizhi, a deceased comprador of Taikoo Dockyard and a native of Chaozhou, resided at No. 10, Lane 177, Luban Road in the French Concession. Gao engaged in a wide range of businesses during his lifetime. His eldest son Gao Yonglian inherited his position as comprador of Taikoo Dockyard. Gao Yonglian was recently sued by his stepmother Gao Bao through attorney Ma Leming in the Civil Court of the Second Special Court for neglecting her livelihood, seeking a judgment ordering the defendant Gao Yonglian to pay sixty yuan per month, amounting to ten years of living expenses. Gao Yonglian himself was summoned to court for verification. The parties arrived in court on time the day before yesterday. First, the plaintiff's attorney stated the previous circumstances. When questioned, the defendant Gao Yonglian stated that his stepmother was cohabiting with a merchant and that all her food and drink were provided by the merchant, so there was no reason to pay her living expenses. The plaintiff claimed that although she had food to eat, she had no vegetables and still needed money for other expenses. At this point, the judge repeatedly advised both parties, and the defendant agreed to pay the plaintiff fifteen yuan per month. Both parties agreed, and a settlement was reached. Report of the Guangdong-Guangxi Industrial Survey Team (3): The Hardworking Guangzhou Bureau of Agriculture and Forestry 122

On the first day of arriving in Guangzhou, I visited Director Feng Rui of the Bureau of Agriculture and Forestry and had a long conversation. Director Feng graduated from the Department of Agriculture at Cornell University and has been working in Ding County, Zhili, as an agricultural expert with great abilities. He first led the survey team to visit the entire bureau. The bureau has an agricultural tool exhibition hall, an industrial testing institute, and a serum manufacturing institute, all of which are excellent. Director Feng said that the province's second phase of economic construction plan is currently being planned, and it is intended to focus on agriculture, such as rice improvement, sugarcane field promotion, aquaculture, animal husbandry, fruit tree propagation, and sideline promotion. After the early rice improvement, the yield can be increased by 25%. Pig, chicken, and duck farming are all starting with improved breeds and increased production. For beekeeping, it is hoped that 5 million beekeeping households will be promoted this year, one hive per household. Sugarcane field management: 15,000 mu are directly managed, and 120,000 mu are contracted sugarcane fields, which can currently meet the needs of the province's six major sugar factories. Director Feng personally went to the Philippines and Java to investigate and research the improvement of sugarcane varieties, bringing back varieties and testing them with good results. Aquaculture focuses on fish diseases and breeding manufacturing, and rice paddy carp farming is strongly promoted. Animal husbandry and veterinary medicine are also training talents and conducting research. Director Feng showed us the recently proposed plan to reduce the province's import surplus, enrich people's lives, and greatly increase production, such as the food production increase plan, the agricultural and animal disease prevention plan, the animal husbandry development plan, the forestry construction plan, the production increase plan, the aquaculture improvement plan, the fruit tree development plan, the tobacco industry revitalization plan, the tea industry development plan, the agricultural irrigation revitalization plan, the new agricultural tool manufacturing plan, the provincial pest control plan, and the wasteland reclamation plan, all with very detailed explanations and estimates. Director Feng gave us numerical instructions when explaining. Before leaving, he gave us many pamphlets. He is a true hardworking person, and we are all impressed. In the evening, Commander-in-Chief Chen Bonan also said in his speech that agriculture is the foundation of industry and commerce. If the countryside is not prosperous and farmers do not have abundant productivity to promote their purchasing power, then urban industry and commerce will never have prosperity. Guangdong Province's hard work today is for a reason.

Strongman at Fu'an Amusement Park Advertises: "Hitting to Death Is Not Compensated" 123

Huang Shigong Was Fooled into Working as a Substitute and Was Hit Until He Vomited Blood

Relatives Learned of This and Went to Investigate, and Both Parties Were Arrested. Huang Shigong, a native of Anhui, thirty-one years old, residing at No. 8, Linjiazhai, Gaochang Temple, and his brother Hongsheng both made a living by sculpting "clay figures." Shigong was strong and powerful, but illiterate. Recently, as life became more difficult, Wang Zhiqing, a strongman from the Xia Ying Martial Arts Troupe at the Fu'an Amusement Park, recruited troupe members to perform fighting ferocious cattle. Huang Shigong was introduced into the troupe. Unexpectedly, Wang Zhiqing advertised widely in newspapers: "Full body 螜螜 kung fu, head, chest, waist, and lower four parts. Please invite the audience to come on stage and test it in person. Hitting to death will not be compensated. This venue is responsible for guaranteeing it." "This venue has a contract of life and death with the strongman." Since Huang Shigong joined the troupe, it has been six days. In Wang Zhiqing's advertisement, the performance of inviting the audience to come on stage to hit him was done by Huang Shigong as a substitute. The day before yesterday, because no audience came on stage, Wang Ruipeng, a strongman from the troupe, hit Huang Shigong more than forty times with an iron plate, causing Huang to be injured and vomit blood. His uncle Zhang Yongqing learned of this. After reviewing the newspapers, he realized that his nephew Huang Shigong had been fooled by Wang Zhiqing. If he was beaten to death, wouldn't he have died in vain? There was an advertisement as proof. Therefore, at 8 PM last night, he gathered Huang's brother Hongsheng and others and went to the Fu'an Amusement Park to ask Wang Zhiqing and the venue manager Bao Qinxuan to read the cattle death contract. Bao replied that this was a game, so an argument broke out, and then a fight broke out. Fortunately, the venue's petition police immediately reported to the Yimiao Police Station by telephone, and a large number of police officers arrived and arrested Wang Ruipeng, Huang Shigong, Huang Hongsheng, Zhang Yongqing, and eight others, bringing them all to the station. They are currently under investigation. If mediation fails, they will be sent to the bureau for interrogation.
